DECLARE @inserted0 TABLE ([Id] int, [_Position] [int]);
MERGE [Products] USING @toInsert0 AS i ON 1=0
WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN
INSERT ([PrimaryProductServerId], [ProductGroup], [ProductName], [SecondaryProductServerId], [TableDataVMId], [TableNumber])
VALUES (i.[PrimaryProductServerId], i.[ProductGroup], i.[ProductName], i.[SecondaryProductServerId], i.[TableDataVMId], i.[TableNumber])
OUTPUT INSERTED.[Id], i._Position
INTO @inserted0;

SELECT [t].[Id] FROM [Products] t
INNER JOIN @inserted0 i ON ([t].[Id] = [i].[Id])
ORDER BY [i].[_Position];

DECLARE @inserted0 TABLE ([Id] int, [_Position] [int]);
MERGE [Products] USING @toInsert0 AS i ON 1=0
WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN
INSERT ([PrimaryProductServerId], [ProductGroup], [ProductName], [SecondaryProductServerId], [TableDataVMId], [TableNumber])
VALUES (i.[PrimaryProductServerId], i.[ProductGroup], i.[ProductName], i.[SecondaryProductServerId], i.[TableDataVMId], i.[TableNumber])
OUTPUT INSERTED.[Id], i._Position
INTO @inserted0;

SELECT [t].[Id] FROM [Products] t
INNER JOIN @inserted0 i ON ([t].[Id] = [i].[Id])
ORDER BY [i].[_Position];

DECLARE @inserted0 TABLE ([Id] int, [_Position] [int]);
MERGE [Servers] USING @toInsert0 AS i ON 1=0
WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN
INSERT ([ServerGroup], [ServerName], [TableDataVMId])
VALUES (i.[ServerGroup], i.[ServerName], i.[TableDataVMId])
OUTPUT INSERTED.[Id], i._Position
INTO @inserted0;

SELECT [t].[Id] FROM [Servers] t
INNER JOIN @inserted0 i ON ([t].[Id] = [i].[Id])
ORDER BY [i].[_Position];
